positive feedback~

negative: This is why I'm giving this place a 2 star out of 5.

When I came to this place, it was very nice looking! I came because I called a few days if I can come in to schedule an appointment, they said sure of course, " can you come on this day.... around this time...?" I agreed. Anyway, I came in, but I had to wait for maybe 30 mins to actually schedule my appointment. I didn't think much about it because I just assume they were busy. *month later.. it's my appointment day*

[Appointment day: Getting my hair done and Makeup]

<Resp>None< /Resp><Pictures>None</Pictures><time>1514332987150</time>< text>
Good sushi for the price, something affordable compared to the plethora of expensive sushi in LA. A nice scene for large groups of post-college aged people, and a good mix of fast food savory and higher quality sushi.
I've lived next to Hara since I was a child, and seen the restaurant evolve and devolve over time. While there have been times where the sushi seemed rushed and low quality shortly after their growth from a hole-in-the-wall to a bigger restaurant, the quality has been consistent for the past 4 years. My main qualm with how the place has grown, is the less social chefs and the random mess of new addition and changes to the menu. There seem to be new sushi rolls with no organization between them, mixing flavors that patrons would only eat on a dare, and having two items that are identical with completely different names. Hara sushi should focus on establishing their menu, rather than changing the name and style of the Wilshire Roll 3 times.</text>

< Review>
As Hara is just a block from my apartment, you can believe that my roommates and I got there quite a bit. The biggest draw is the price: you get pretty good sushi for a low price, not to mention good, LARGE, Japanese beers.

I definitely recommend Hara for a fun happy hour experience, and (bonus) the deals aren't limited to certain hours of the day. The hand rolls are the way to go: lots of fish in a neatly wrapped package. Their specialty rolls are also yummy, especially the caterpillar. Also, big bonus points for the included miso soups with food orders.

The service is always prompt, but there can be a wait at peak hours (5-8). Don't forget to bring cash for a 10% discount!< /Review>

<Text>I'm addicted!

I really love coming here to have some sushi and Saporro. The prices are great and the sushi rolls I always get are delicious.

I've tried different rolls, but over time I only order two of my favorite ones to share. The Lighthouse Roll and the Wilshire Roll.

The Lighthouse Roll is yummy and unique. It has a citrus lime taste that I absolutely love!!!
The Wilshire Roll is similar to a baby lobster roll at other restaurants. I like it because its good and filling.
I highly recommend both of these if you are undecided. They will not let you down.

The beers are cheap. My favorite is a Saporro and it goes perfect with the sushi rolls.

I love that everyone always starts off with Miso soup and ends with complimentary green tea ice cream. I leave a happy customer every time.

Hara can get very loud at night with tons of customers coming in and out. Sometimes you'll have to wait to be seated but its worth it. I personally love the atmosphere and young faces. Customer service is pretty good too.<//Text><Pictures>None</Pictures><resp>None</resp>< gmap_id>

<Review>My husband and I are in santa monica for one night, before we fly out to Tahiti tomorrow. We both had a craving for sushi, seeing as their is a sushi restaurant on almost every corner in the LA area. I researched and read reviews,and looked for a place that would stay open past 9pm. We chose hara and I am so so glad we did! The BEST sushi/sashimi I've had in a long time. My fav is salmon and yellowtail, which were both incredibly fresh and prepared just right.. but we had 2 kinds of tuna as well,which were also perfect.
The rolls were great also! I suggest the terminator. We both loved every single thing we ordered! And the price is much more affordable than our regular spots in dallas/fortworth. The service was on point, the food came out incredibly fast,and the manager even came over to make sure we were satisfied before we left. When we return to LA, we will forever make time to go eat at hara again. Thanks to everyone there. This was our first dinner together as a married couple and it was amazing.< /Review><Pictures>None</Pictures>< resp>

< review>
In a league of their own, bar none!

Nothing about this establishment says, pawn shop. I was referred to this location when, and if, I was interested in selling any of my 1oz gold coins or intrigued to obtaining some new ones. Upon entering and soaking it in, I felt as if I was inside a upscale boutique (Chanel) inside Nordstrom at South Coast Plaza mall. Made me scratch my head and check that I was in the right store. ü§î

Fine jewelry, high end watches (ie: Chopard), unique diamond pieces, rare collectables and the back wall dripping from top to bottom in high end designer handbags and men's wallets from LV. In addition, Posh Pawn utilizes a handheld device developed by Entrupy, Inc. that microscopically detects the convincing fakes out there, from the 100% authentic. Very cool!

Overall, beautiful merchandise in nearly mint condition! LV messenger bag with proof of purchase, as if the owner didn't even use it after spending close to $3k! üòÆ

Btw... April, Thomas, Kermit the Frog and the Habib guy... Don't know what they're on but they need to know that drugs are bad! If they weren't on them, they would see more clearly!

Paola (I think that was her name) effortlessly oozes professionalism and class.

I will make another visit after leaving NYC for the holidays.
San Diego is lucky to have them (Pugsie would agree). Posh indeed!< /review>

1) No assigned parking, and we could never find parking spot. Because of this, we sold one of our cars. If you like to have your own parking spot, it will cost you $100 for reserving a parking spot. We ever saw one car with no wheels, because the tires were all stolen. Wow!

2) Fire alarm constantly went off, and it is very annoying to all the residents. The only explanation was the alarm system malfunctioned in some ways, but still the fire alarm kept going off for months. It even happened during mid night around 2-3 am, and lasted for about 30 min or longer. The staff just said that some residents smoked inside of their place, which caused the fire alarm to go off. So nothing much they can do to fix this issue. Does that mean we are paying the rent for some people to cause the fire alarm to go off to ruin our sleep? If you have a baby, this is a big no no.

3) We requested for window screen installation several times and it took about 4 months to get it done. I am pretty sure that the apartment has a lot of requests for window installation.
In addition to that, the service staff entered our apartment without having us on site. What if something valuable is missing, who will be responsible for it?

We just want them to fix  the problem, but the problems are always there. I know every apartment has its problems, but they always try to fix it. Apparently not this apartment.

< text>
We have a tankless hot water heater - it worked fine for several years and then started randomly shutting off.  I had called the company who installed it, they charged me almost $500 to "clean" the unit but the problem still was not fixed.   I called another plumber who supposedly worked on tankless hot water heaters - they also tried to fix the problem by "cleaning" the unit, more money spent and still not fixed.   I was about ready to have the unit replaced and install a new unit, but AirStream Heating and Air happened to be working on my furnace - I asked them if they could recommend someone, they gave me the name of Patriot Plumbing.   Basically, Patriot came out spent a few minutes on the phone with the tankless manufacturer and discovered that the altitude had never been set correctly on the unit - set the correct altitude and presto every thing worked again as advertised.   Patriot charged me a responsible rate for fixing the problem, at about a quarter of the previous two plumbers - but the tankless water heater worked fine after they left and is still working fine several years later!   Highly recommend Patriot - they have since fixed several other plumbing issues at our house and office, each time with great service.   Can't say enough good about these folks!< /text>

<Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
To compete with Black Angus restaurant, the Outback has steak and seafood specials that blow them away.  The steaks are noticably better quality and way more tender than at Black Angus.  The seafood is better than at Red Lobster. The servers are super friendly and eager to make suggestions.  If you are lucky your server will be Victor G.  He is the best server we've had in 10 years, not just at the Outback.  He treats you like you are at a five star gourmet restaurant.  If the Outback is smart they will promote Victor so he will be the regional trainer of all new servers, followed by managing his own restaurant.  He takes pride in his work and does his best to please you.  That's something I've never seen at a chain restaurant.< /Review>
